end function Hop()local d=game.PlaceId local s={}local V=""local Y=(os.date("!*t")).hour local N=false function TPReturner()local N if V~=""then N=game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"..(d..("/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100&cursor="..V))))else N=game.HttpService:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/"..(d.."/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100")))end local w=""if N.nextPageCursor and(N.nextPageCursor~="null"and N.nextPageCursor~="null")then V=N.nextPageCursor end local E=0 for V,N in pairs(N.data)do local I=true w=tostring(N.id)if tonumber(N.maxPlayers)>tonumber(N.playing)then for d,V in pairs(s)do if E~=0 then if w==tostring(V)then I=false end elseif tonumber(Y)~=tonumber(V)then local d=pcall(function()s={}table.insert(s,Y)end)end E=E+1 end if I==true then table.insert(s,w)wait(.1)pcall(function()wait();(game:GetService("TeleportService")):TeleportToPlaceInstance(d,w,game.Players.LocalPlayer)end)wait(.1)end end end end function Teleport()while wait(.1)do pcall(function()TPReturner()if V~=""then TPReturner()end end)end end Teleport()end function CheckItem(d)for s,V in pairs((game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")).Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory"))do if V.Name==d then return V end end end function UpdateIslandESP()for d,s in pairs((game:GetService("Workspace"))._WorldOrigin.Locations:GetChildren())do do local d=s pcall(function()if IslandESP then if d.Name~="Sea"then if not d:FindFirstChild("NameEsp")then local s=Instance.new("BillboardGui",d)s.Name="NameEsp"s.ExtentsOffset=Vector3.new(0,1,0)s.Size=UDim2.new(1,200,1,30)s.Adornee=d s.AlwaysOnTop=true local
